<h1 className={"openapi__heading"}>Resolve Functions</h1>

<MethodEndpoint method={"post"} path={"/api/v32.06/serverless/evaluate"}></MethodEndpoint>



```
x-prisma-cloud-target-env: {"permission":"monitorCI"}
x-public: true
```



Adds vulnerability data for the given functions.

## Request
